docs/0.17.0/_sources/parameters.rst.txt:    p2 = Params(name="two_gpus", num_gpus=2)
docs/0.17.0/_sources/parameters.rst.txt:sets of outputs. However, we may want to change the number of gpus we use (when moving between
docs/0.17.0/_sources/parameters.rst.txt:If we want to ignore ``num_gpus``, it might look like this:
docs/0.17.0/_sources/parameters.rst.txt:        num_gpus: int = 1
docs/0.17.0/_sources/parameters.rst.txt:        hash_representations: dict = cf.set_hash_functions(num_gpus=None)
docs/0.17.0/_sources/parameters.rst.txt:    p1 = Params(name="one_gpu", num_gpus=1)
docs/0.17.0/_sources/parameters.rst.txt:    p2 = Params(name="two_gpus", num_gpus=2)
docs/0.17.0/_sources/parameters.rst.txt:representation on num_gpus:
docs/0.17.0/_sources/parameters.rst.txt:        num_gpus: int = 1
docs/0.17.0/_sources/parameters.rst.txt:            num_gpus=None,
docs/0.17.0/_sources/parameters.rst.txt:            model_size=lambda self, obj: str(obj/self.num_gpus)
docs/0.17.0/_sources/parameters.rst.txt:    p1 = Params(name="one_gpu", model_size=4500, num_gpus=1)
docs/0.17.0/_sources/parameters.rst.txt:    p2 = Params(name="two_gpus", model_size=9000, num_gpus=2)
